Here is the situation:\\ \tt \\ \tt WHAT: Things at places\\ \tt LEFT: dog\\ \tt RIGHT: jacket\\ \tt TOP: cat\\ \tt BOTTOM: skirts\\ \tt CENTER: plate\\ \tt NORTHWEST: melons\\ \tt NORTHEAST: helium\\ \tt SOUTHWEST: evening gown\\ \tt SOUTHEAST: bikini\\ \tt HERE: jeans skirt\\ \tt THERE: camellia\\ \tt NOWHERE: clips\\ \tt EVERYWHERE: table mat\\ \tt INSIDE: tuba\\ \tt OUTSIDE: post-it notes\\ \tt \\ \tt Questions from the questioner will start with QUESTIONER. Please reply in the form: ANSWER: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt I will also ask you questions. These questions will start with ME: . Please answer these questions with: ASIDE: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt Important: Give short, direct answers!\\ \tt \\ \tt Let us start.
